SonghayCore\r","\r","[![Build Status](https://songhay.visualstudio.com/SonghaySystem/_apis/build/status/songhay-core-yaml-build?branchName=master)](https://songhay.visualstudio.com/SonghaySystem/_build/latest?definitionId=16\u0026branchName=master)\r","\r","Here is the _Core_ code to install as [a NuGet package](https://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore/) for all of my studio Solutions. Anyone who may be reading this 👀 is free to do the same. This package is based on `net8.0`.\r","\r","**NuGet package 📦:** [`SonghayCore`](https://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore/)\r","\r","**documentation 📚:** [`SonghayCore` API](https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/)\r","\r","## _core_ reusable, opinionated concerns\r","\r","### `Songhay.Hosting`\r","\r","One of the most important additions to .NET came in .NET 6.0 (circa 2021): the _.NET Generic Host_ [📖 [docs](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/generic-host)]. This _host_ concept from Microsoft allows developers to _not_ have to reinvent:\r","\r","- Dependency injection (DI)\r","- Logging\r","- Configuration\r","- App shutdown\r","- `IHostedService` implementations (for long-running background tasks \\[📖 [docs](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/timer-service?pivots=dotnet-7-0) \\])\r","\r","All ASP.NET developers expect to get these things “for free” and, finally, Microsoft is basically letting all .NET developers get these things for free. This _Core_ recognizes the _.NET Generic Host_, stating with the `DefaultHostedService` [class](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Hosting/DefaultHostedService.cs) (see `Songhay.Extensions` below for more details).\r","\r","### `Songhay.Diagnostics`\r","\r","This _Core_ is concerned with _tracing_ as well as logging. Logging concerns should be logically above this _Core_. [`TraceSources`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Diagnostics/TraceSources.cs) and [`TraceSourceExtensions`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/TraceSourceExtensions.cs) define how tracing should be implemented with a bias toward using all source levels. When tracing is not configured for this _Core_ then it will be ignored without throwing exceptions.\r","\r","For a review of the organizational difference between tracing and logging, see “[Tracing vs Logging vs Monitoring: What’s the Difference?](https://www.bmc.com/blogs/monitoring-logging-tracing/)” by [Chrissy Kidd](https://www.linkedin.com/in/chrissy-k-47294593).\r","\r","**Documentation 📚:** [`Songhay.Diagnostics`](https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Diagnostics/)\r","\r","### `Songhay.Extensions`\r","\r","The Songhay System uses imperative C# code with a view to make it more functional in an effort to control complexity and enhance maintainability.\r","\r","The preference for [extension methods](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/tree/master/SonghayCore/Extensions) encourages stateless, reusable routines (many of them are “pure” functions).\r","\r","Notable extensions:\r","\r","- [`IConfigurationExtensions`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/IConfigurationExtensions.cs) — defines shared routines based on conventions around the _.NET Generic Host_ [📖 [docs](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/generic-host)].\r","\r","- [`IConfigurationBuilderExtensions`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/IConfigurationBuilderExtensions.cs) — defines shared routines for application configuration building under .NET Standard.\r","\r","- [`ILoggerExtensions`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/ILoggerExtensions.cs) — defines shared routines based on conventions around the _.NET Generic Host_ [📖 [docs](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/generic-host)].\r","\r","- [`HttpRequestMessageExtensions`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/HttpRequestMessageExtensions.cs) — defines shared routines for HTTP access under .NET Standard with a lazy-loaded `HttpClient`. Routines for Azure Blob Storage are included here.\r","\r","- [`HttpWebRequestExtensions`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/HttpWebRequestExtensions.cs) — defines shared routines for HTTP access for the legacy .NET Framework.\r","\r","There is support for [URI templates](http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6570) (to be used with [`RestApiMetadata`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/RestApiMetadata.cs)) in the form of [extension methods](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/RestApiMetadataExtensions.Tavis.cs), running on top of [`Tavis.UriTemplates`](https://github.com/tavis-software/Tavis.UriTemplates).\r","\r","**Documentation 📚:** [`Songhay.Extensions`](https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Extensions/)\r","\r","### `Songhay.Models`\r","\r","The _Core_ models of the Songhay System define types for MIME, XHTML, OPML, REST, the Repository, the Display Item (for WPF and other MVVM solutions), etc.\r","\r","The _Core_ models are “anemic” by design (there are very few abstract classes)—any logic would be found _first_ in an Extension Method.\r","\r","Notable models:\r","\r","- [`DisplayItemModel`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/DisplayItemModel.cs) — defines the conventional way to display data.\r","\r","- [`MenuDisplayItemModel`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/MenuDisplayItemModel.cs) — defines the conventional way to display nested/grouped data.\r","\r","- [`RestApiMetadata`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/RestApiMetadata.cs) — defines conventional REST API metadata.\r","\r","**Documentation 📚:** [`Songhay.Models`](https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Models/)\r","\r","### `Songhay.Xml`\r","\r","The “core” of the _Core_ is concern for XML. The Songhay System started out as utilities around [`XPathDocument`](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.xml.xpath.xpathdocument(v=vs.110).aspx) and grew into LINQ for XML—over [`XDocument`](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.xml.linq.xdocument(v=vs.110).aspx).\r","\r","**Documentation 📚:** [`Songhay.Xml`](https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Xml/)\r","\r","## fundamental boundary-crossing abstractions\r","\r","This _Core_ features the ‘boundary-crossing abstractions’ (and default implementations) needed for the enterprise work based on my historical needs:\r","\r","- [`IApiEndpoint`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IApiEndpoint.cs) — defines the conventional way to access distributed data (default implementation: [`ApiEndpoint`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/ApiEndpoint.cs)).\r","- [`IApiRequestStrategy`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IApiRequestStrategy.cs) — defines the conventional way to request data from an endpoint (default implementations: [`ApiRequestStrategy`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/ApiRequestStrategy.cs) and [`AzureBlobApiRequestStrategy`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/AzureBlobApiRequestStrategy.cs)).\r","- [`IBlobStreamApiEndpoint`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IBlobStreamApiEndpoint.cs) — defines the conventional way to request BLOB data from an endpoint (default implementation: [`BlobStreamApiEndpoint`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/BlobStreamApiEndpoint.cs)).\r","\r","Dependency-injecting these ‘boundary-crossing abstractions’ are far more mockable than, say, using `HttpRequestMessage` directly.\r","\r","## the _core_ Activity concept\r","\r","This _Core_ features the concept of the Activity which is a way to formally recognize that all line of business applications can be thought of as a ‘tree’ of inputs and outputs. It follows that each ‘node’ of this ‘tree’ can be called an Activity. The following abstractions classify the Activities needed so far:\r","\r","- [`IActivity`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivity.cs) — defines the conventional, synchronous, input-output Activities\r","- [`IActivityOutputOnly`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivityOutputOnly.cs) — defines the conventional, synchronous Activities with output only (input usually comes from `IConfiguration` in this case)\r","- [`IActivityOutputOnlyTask`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivityOutputOnlyTask.cs) — defines the conventional, asynchronous Activities with output only (input usually comes from `IConfiguration` in this case)\r","- [`IActivityTask`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivityTask.cs) — defines the conventional, asynchronous, input-output Activities\r","\r","This Activity concept which I regard as _fundamental_ is the least likely architectural reality that would be shared by my peers 😐 From the Microsoft point of view, my Activity concept would be buried under [Windows Workflow Foundation](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Windows_Workflow_Foundation) or [BizTalk Server](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft_BizTalk_Server).\r","\r","## satellite packages\r","\r","### `SonghayCore.xUnit`\r","\r","Defines reusable class definitions for [xUnit](https://xunit.net/). Featured is the [`ProjectFileDataAttribute`](https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore.xUnit/ProjectFileDataAttribute.cs), allowing test data files to be loaded from a relative path.\r","\r","**NuGet package 📦:** [`SonghayCore.xUnit`](http://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore.xUnit/)\r","\r","**Documentation 📚:** [`Songhay.Tests`](https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Tests/)\r","\r","### `SonghayCore.Newtonsoft`\r","\r","Core reusable, opinionated Newtonsoft concerns for my C# projects.\r","\r","**GitHub repo:** \u003chttps://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore.Newtonsoft\u003e\r","\r","**NuGet package 📦:** [`SonghayCore.Newtonsoft`](https://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore.Newtonsoft/)\r","\r","## Studio packages dependent on `SonghayCore`\r","\r","```mermaid\r","graph BT\r","    netstandard2[.NET aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="BlobContent-module__blobContentSection__VOgZq BlobContent-module__blobContentSectionMarkdown__mPLOK" style="margin-top:46px"><div class="Box-sc-62in7e-0 js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned BlobContent-module__markdownBlob__T8jpG" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SonghayCore</h1><a id="user-content-songhaycore" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SonghayCore" href="#songhaycore"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://songhay.visualstudio.com/SonghaySystem/_build/latest?definitionId=16&amp;branchName=master" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/5cca85097c88b8363517c8b953036bbd1988241137a193070127fed15ca8a54f/68747470733a2f2f736f6e676861792e76697375616c73747564696f2e636f6d2f536f6e6768617953797374656d2f5f617069732f6275696c642f7374617475732f736f6e676861792d636f72652d79616d6c2d6275696c643f6272616e63684e616d653d6d6173746572" alt="Build Status" data-canonical-src="https://songhay.visualstudio.com/SonghaySystem/_apis/build/status/songhay-core-yaml-build?branchName=master" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Here is the <em>Core</em> code to install as <a href="https://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore/" rel="nofollow">a NuGet package</a> for all of my studio Solutions. Anyone who may be reading this 👀 is free to do the same. This package is based on <code>net8.0</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NuGet package 📦:</strong> <a href="https://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore/" rel="nofollow"><code>SonghayCore</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>documentation 📚:</strong> <a href="https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/" rel="nofollow"><code>SonghayCore</code> API</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><em>core</em> reusable, opinionated concerns</h2><a id="user-content-core-reusable-opinionated-concerns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: core reusable, opinionated concerns" href="#core-reusable-opinionated-concerns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>Songhay.Hosting</code></h3><a id="user-content-songhayhosting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Songhay.Hosting" href="#songhayhosting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">One of the most important additions to .NET came in .NET 6.0 (circa 2021): the <em>.NET Generic Host</em> [📖 <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/generic-host" rel="nofollow">docs</a>]. This <em>host</em> concept from Microsoft allows developers to <em>not</em> have to reinvent:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Dependency injection (DI)</li>
<li>Logging</li>
<li>Configuration</li>
<li>App shutdown</li>
<li><code>IHostedService</code> implementations (for long-running background tasks [📖 <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/timer-service?pivots=dotnet-7-0" rel="nofollow">docs</a> ])</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">All ASP.NET developers expect to get these things “for free” and, finally, Microsoft is basically letting all .NET developers get these things for free. This <em>Core</em> recognizes the <em>.NET Generic Host</em>, stating with the <code>DefaultHostedService</code> <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Hosting/DefaultHostedService.cs">class</a> (see <code>Songhay.Extensions</code> below for more details).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>Songhay.Diagnostics</code></h3><a id="user-content-songhaydiagnostics" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Songhay.Diagnostics" href="#songhaydiagnostics"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This <em>Core</em> is concerned with <em>tracing</em> as well as logging. Logging concerns should be logically above this <em>Core</em>. <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Diagnostics/TraceSources.cs"><code>TraceSources</code></a> and <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/TraceSourceExtensions.cs"><code>TraceSourceExtensions</code></a> define how tracing should be implemented with a bias toward using all source levels. When tracing is not configured for this <em>Core</em> then it will be ignored without throwing exceptions.</p>
<p dir="auto">For a review of the organizational difference between tracing and logging, see “<a href="https://www.bmc.com/blogs/monitoring-logging-tracing/" rel="nofollow">Tracing vs Logging vs Monitoring: What’s the Difference?</a>” by <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/chrissy-k-47294593" rel="nofollow">Chrissy Kidd</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Documentation 📚:</strong> <a href="https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Diagnostics/" rel="nofollow"><code>Songhay.Diagnostics</code></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>Songhay.Extensions</code></h3><a id="user-content-songhayextensions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Songhay.Extensions" href="#songhayextensions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Songhay System uses imperative C# code with a view to make it more functional in an effort to control complexity and enhance maintainability.</p>
<p dir="auto">The preference for <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/tree/master/SonghayCore/Extensions">extension methods</a> encourages stateless, reusable routines (many of them are “pure” functions).</p>
<p dir="auto">Notable extensions:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/IConfigurationExtensions.cs"><code>IConfigurationExtensions</code></a> — defines shared routines based on conventions around the <em>.NET Generic Host</em> [📖 <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/generic-host" rel="nofollow">docs</a>].</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/IConfigurationBuilderExtensions.cs"><code>IConfigurationBuilderExtensions</code></a> — defines shared routines for application configuration building under .NET Standard.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/ILoggerExtensions.cs"><code>ILoggerExtensions</code></a> — defines shared routines based on conventions around the <em>.NET Generic Host</em> [📖 <a href="https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/core/extensions/generic-host" rel="nofollow">docs</a>].</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/HttpRequestMessageExtensions.cs"><code>HttpRequestMessageExtensions</code></a> — defines shared routines for HTTP access under .NET Standard with a lazy-loaded <code>HttpClient</code>. Routines for Azure Blob Storage are included here.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/HttpWebRequestExtensions.cs"><code>HttpWebRequestExtensions</code></a> — defines shared routines for HTTP access for the legacy .NET Framework.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">There is support for <a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6570" rel="nofollow">URI templates</a> (to be used with <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/RestApiMetadata.cs"><code>RestApiMetadata</code></a>) in the form of <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Extensions/RestApiMetadataExtensions.Tavis.cs">extension methods</a>, running on top of <a href="https://github.com/tavis-software/Tavis.UriTemplates"><code>Tavis.UriTemplates</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Documentation 📚:</strong> <a href="https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Extensions/" rel="nofollow"><code>Songhay.Extensions</code></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>Songhay.Models</code></h3><a id="user-content-songhaymodels" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Songhay.Models" href="#songhaymodels"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <em>Core</em> models of the Songhay System define types for MIME, XHTML, OPML, REST, the Repository, the Display Item (for WPF and other MVVM solutions), etc.</p>
<p dir="auto">The <em>Core</em> models are “anemic” by design (there are very few abstract classes)—any logic would be found <em>first</em> in an Extension Method.</p>
<p dir="auto">Notable models:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/DisplayItemModel.cs"><code>DisplayItemModel</code></a> — defines the conventional way to display data.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/MenuDisplayItemModel.cs"><code>MenuDisplayItemModel</code></a> — defines the conventional way to display nested/grouped data.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Models/RestApiMetadata.cs"><code>RestApiMetadata</code></a> — defines conventional REST API metadata.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Documentation 📚:</strong> <a href="https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Models/" rel="nofollow"><code>Songhay.Models</code></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>Songhay.Xml</code></h3><a id="user-content-songhayxml" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Songhay.Xml" href="#songhayxml"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The “core” of the <em>Core</em> is concern for XML. The Songhay System started out as utilities around <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.xml.xpath.xpathdocument(v=vs.110).aspx" rel="nofollow"><code>XPathDocument</code></a> and grew into LINQ for XML—over <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/system.xml.linq.xdocument(v=vs.110).aspx" rel="nofollow"><code>XDocument</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Documentation 📚:</strong> <a href="https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Xml/" rel="nofollow"><code>Songhay.Xml</code></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">fundamental boundary-crossing abstractions</h2><a id="user-content-fundamental-boundary-crossing-abstractions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: fundamental boundary-crossing abstractions" href="#fundamental-boundary-crossing-abstractions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This <em>Core</em> features the ‘boundary-crossing abstractions’ (and default implementations) needed for the enterprise work based on my historical needs:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IApiEndpoint.cs"><code>IApiEndpoint</code></a> — defines the conventional way to access distributed data (default implementation: <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/ApiEndpoint.cs"><code>ApiEndpoint</code></a>).</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IApiRequestStrategy.cs"><code>IApiRequestStrategy</code></a> — defines the conventional way to request data from an endpoint (default implementations: <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/ApiRequestStrategy.cs"><code>ApiRequestStrategy</code></a> and <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/AzureBlobApiRequestStrategy.cs"><code>AzureBlobApiRequestStrategy</code></a>).</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IBlobStreamApiEndpoint.cs"><code>IBlobStreamApiEndpoint</code></a> — defines the conventional way to request BLOB data from an endpoint (default implementation: <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Net/BlobStreamApiEndpoint.cs"><code>BlobStreamApiEndpoint</code></a>).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Dependency-injecting these ‘boundary-crossing abstractions’ are far more mockable than, say, using <code>HttpRequestMessage</code> directly.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">the <em>core</em> Activity concept</h2><a id="user-content-the-core-activity-concept" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: the core Activity concept" href="#the-core-activity-concept"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This <em>Core</em> features the concept of the Activity which is a way to formally recognize that all line of business applications can be thought of as a ‘tree’ of inputs and outputs. It follows that each ‘node’ of this ‘tree’ can be called an Activity. The following abstractions classify the Activities needed so far:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivity.cs"><code>IActivity</code></a> — defines the conventional, synchronous, input-output Activities</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivityOutputOnly.cs"><code>IActivityOutputOnly</code></a> — defines the conventional, synchronous Activities with output only (input usually comes from <code>IConfiguration</code> in this case)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivityOutputOnlyTask.cs"><code>IActivityOutputOnlyTask</code></a> — defines the conventional, asynchronous Activities with output only (input usually comes from <code>IConfiguration</code> in this case)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore/Abstractions/IActivityTask.cs"><code>IActivityTask</code></a> — defines the conventional, asynchronous, input-output Activities</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">This Activity concept which I regard as <em>fundamental</em> is the least likely architectural reality that would be shared by my peers 😐 From the Microsoft point of view, my Activity concept would be buried under <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Windows_Workflow_Foundation" rel="nofollow">Windows Workflow Foundation</a> or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft_BizTalk_Server" rel="nofollow">BizTalk Server</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">satellite packages</h2><a id="user-content-satellite-packages" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: satellite packages" href="#satellite-packages"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>SonghayCore.xUnit</code></h3><a id="user-content-songhaycorexunit" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SonghayCore.xUnit" href="#songhaycorexunit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Defines reusable class definitions for <a href="https://xunit.net/" rel="nofollow">xUnit</a>. Featured is the <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore/blob/master/SonghayCore.xUnit/ProjectFileDataAttribute.cs"><code>ProjectFileDataAttribute</code></a>, allowing test data files to be loaded from a relative path.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NuGet package 📦:</strong> <a href="http://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore.xUnit/" rel="nofollow"><code>SonghayCore.xUnit</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Documentation 📚:</strong> <a href="https://bryanwilhite.github.io/SonghayCore/latest/Songhay.Tests/" rel="nofollow"><code>Songhay.Tests</code></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>SonghayCore.Newtonsoft</code></h3><a id="user-content-songhaycorenewtonsoft" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SonghayCore.Newtonsoft" href="#songhaycorenewtonsoft"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Core reusable, opinionated Newtonsoft concerns for my C# projects.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>GitHub repo:</strong> <a href="https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore.Newtonsoft">https://github.com/BryanWilhite/SonghayCore.Newtonsoft</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NuGet package 📦:</strong> <a href="https://www.nuget.org/packages/SonghayCore.Newtonsoft/" rel="nofollow"><code>SonghayCore.Newtonsoft</code></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Studio packages dependent on <code>SonghayCore</code></h2><a id="user-content-studio-packages-dependent-on-songhaycore" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Studio packages dependent on SonghayCore" href="#studio-packages-dependent-on-songhaycore"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
